    <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">var HkjcWebUrl = '//www.hkjc.com';
var JcrwUrlPrefix = '/racing/Info';
var ajaxBeforeSendTip = '<div style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; text-align:center;">Processing...</div><br/>';
var ajaxErrorTip = '<div style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; text-align:center;">Network or system busy, please try again later. Sorry for the inconveniences caused.</div><br/>';
var jsController = 'race';
var jsAction = 'exceptionalfactors';
var jsJcerwWebUrl = '//racing.hkjc.com/racing/info';
var jsJCRWDomainIP = 'racing.hkjc.com';
var jsJCEWDomainIP = 'www.hkjc.com';
var curIsEnglish = true;
var curIsSimulcast = false;
var wcmsUrlPrefix = '//racing.hkjc.com/racing/overseas';
var preUrl = '/racing/info/meeting/ExceptionalFactors/English/Local/20090118/ST/03';
var maxRetryCount = 4;
var delayTime = '2000';
var JcrwSSOPath = '//racing.hkjc.com/racing/jcrw/';
var SSOCommonPath = '//common.hkjc.com/corporate/';
var SearchPath = '//search.hkjc.com';
var hidePanel = false;
var JCRWSystemCutoffDate = '20110815';
var PageIsReady = true;
var jsPageType = '';
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var curStatus = null;

        function toggleLang() {
            var curURL = document.URL;  //document.location.href;
            var isLOHEngChiArt = false; //Check if it is E_ or C_ type categories 
            if (arguments.length > 0) {
                curURL = arguments[0];
            }

            var regExpStr = '(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
            if (jsController == 'latestonhorse') {
                switch (jsAction) {
                    case 'index':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        break;
                    case 'show':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/tp50|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/csum|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/smon|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/clas)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';

			if (curURL.indexOf('_ahrl') >= 0) {
                            regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/[e|c]_ahrl)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                            jsPageType = curURL.indexOf('e_ahrl') ? 'e_ahrl' : 'c_ahrl';
                            isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                        }

                        break;
                    case 'list':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        switch (jsPageType.substr(0, 2)) {
                            case 'e_':
                            case 'c_':
                                regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                                isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                                break;
                        }
                        break;
                }
            }

            //var reg = new RegExp('(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?', 'i');
            var reg = new RegExp(regExpStr, 'i');
            var idx = curURL.match(reg);
            if (idx != null) {
                var urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                var urlLang = RegExp.$2;
                var urlPara = RegExp.$3;

                //If categories under LatestOnHorse is with E_ or C_, refine the curURL for the lang link in header
                if (isLOHEngChiArt) {                    
                        urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                        urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(curIsEnglish ? '/c_' : '/e_');
			urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(jsPageType.substr(2, jsPageType.length));
			if (jsAction == "list"){
                        	urlPrefix = urlPrefix + '/list';
			}
                        urlLang = RegExp.$3;
                        urlPara = RegExp.$4;                    
                }
                
                if (urlLang == null || urlLang == '' || urlLang.toLowerCase() == '/chinese') {
                    urlLang = '/English';
                }
                else {
                    urlLang = '/Chinese';
                }
                curURL = urlPrefix + urlLang + urlPara;                
            }
            
            $("#topNav a.lang").attr("href", curURL);
        }

        function ajaxNav(url) {
            $.ajax({
                url: url,
                data: { "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest" },
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "html",
                beforeSend: function() {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxBeforeSendTip);
                },
                error: function() {
                    //ajax error
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                },
                success: function(data) {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(data);
                    //for change the language
                    toggleLang(url);
                    //for Image roll over
                    rolloverInit();

                    //not ready for ajax loading
                    if ($('.mainError').length > 0) {

                        curStatus = $("#hidStatus").val();
                        if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                            window.location = url; //refresh the url and use reload approach                                                
                        } else { //ERROR or ...
                            $(".mainError").show();
                            if (curIsSimulcast) {
                                changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                            }
                        }

                    } //endif
                }
            });
        }

        function AutoReload(retryCount) {
            if (retryCount < maxRetryCount) {
                Reload = setTimeout(function() {
                    $.ajax({
                        cache: false,
                        url: preUrl,
                        type: "POST",
                        dataType: "html",
                        error: function() {
                            //ajax error
                            $("#loading").hide();
                            $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                        },
                        success: function(data) {
                            if (data.indexOf("mainError") > 0 && data.indexOf('Redirect') <= 0) {
                                if (data.indexOf('value="ERROR"') > 0) {
                                    retryCount = maxRetryCount;
                                }
                                AutoReload(retryCount + 1);

                            } else {
                                //reset the retry count
                                retryCount = 0;

                                //Data is OK,  and display it!;
                                //Fix the invalidation of js function after update by Ajax
                                window.location = preUrl;
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }, delayTime);
            } else {
                if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                    $(".retryLink").show();
                }

                $("#loading").hide();
                if (hidePanel) {
                    $("#divRemark").show();
                } else {
                    $(".mainError").show();
                    if (curIsSimulcast) {
                        changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                    }
                }
                if (parent.document.location.href.toLowerCase().indexOf(wcmsUrlPrefix) < 0) {
                    try {
                        WATracker.trackPageView('racing-content');
                    } catch (e) {
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

<!-- script for search box -->
<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
   var focus = "false";
   var search_category = "racing";
   document.getElementById("searchtext").onkeypress = function handleKeyPress(evt){
   var keycode = (window.event)?event.keyCode:evt.which;
	   if(keycode == 13){
		  if(isFocus){
			   focus = "false";
			   goSearch();
			   focus = "true";

		  }
  }
   }
   function replaceAllChar(text, inp) {
	   while(text.indexOf(inp)>=0)
		   text = text.replace(inp, '');
	   return text;
   }
   function goSearch(){

	 if( focus == "false") {

	 var keyword = document.getElementById('searchtext').value;
	 for (var i=0; i<charArr.length; i++)                 
		 keyword = replaceAllChar(keyword, charArr[i]);
	 keyword = keyword.replace(/^\s+/, '').replace(/\s+$/, '');    
	 if(keyword == "" || keyword == "Search" || keyword == "搜尋"){

	 var lang =  "english";
	
	 if(lang == "english")
	alert("Please input a search query");

	 if(lang == "chinese")
			 alert("請輸入搜尋字串");
	}
	else {
		//	+ SearchPath
		  var url = SearchPath + "/search/english/search.aspx?k="+Base64.encode(encodeURIComponent(keyword));
		  if(search_category=="utility"){
			   url += "&g=faq";
		  }
		  else{
			   url += "&g=all";
		  }
		  url += "&t=n";
		  window.location.href = url;
	   }
 }
 else {
		 focus = "false";
	}
 }
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    //add selected effect
    $("#navmenu-h a").filter(function() {
        return this.href.toLowerCase().indexOf("/" + jsController.replace("race", "meeting") + "/" + jsAction) > -1;
    }).addClass("selected");
    //add arrow gif
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").filter(function() {
        return $(this).find("ul").length > 0;
    }).prepend("<div class='navmenu-arrow' />");
    //adjust position of sub menu
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").hover(function() {
        if (document.body.clientWidth < ($(this).offset().left + 400)) {
            $(this).find("ul").css("left", "-101%");
        }
    }, function() {
        $(this).find("ul").css("left", "100%");
    });    
</script>

        height += $(this).children("li").filter(".multirow3").length * 30;
        return $("<div class='navmenu-shadow' />").height(height);
    });

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">

function getURLType() {
    var url = window.location;
    var localPattern = /racing\/info/i;
    var overseaPattern = /racing\/overseas/i;
    if (localPattern.test(url)) {
        return "local";
    }
    else if (overseaPattern.test(url)) {
        return "overseas";
    }
    else {
        return "na";
    }
}

var maxRetryCount = 4;
var delayTime = '2000';

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var curStatus = null;

        function toggleLang() {
            var curURL = document.URL;  //document.location.href;
            var isLOHEngChiArt = false; //Check if it is E_ or C_ type categories 
            if (arguments.length > 0) {
                curURL = arguments[0];
            }

            var regExpStr = '(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
            if (jsController == 'latestonhorse') {
                switch (jsAction) {
                    case 'index':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        break;
                    case 'show':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/tp50|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/csum|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/smon|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/clas)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';

			if (curURL.indexOf('_ahrl') >= 0) {
                            regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/[e|c]_ahrl)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                            jsPageType = curURL.indexOf('e_ahrl') ? 'e_ahrl' : 'c_ahrl';
                            isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                        }

                        break;
                    case 'list':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        switch (jsPageType.substr(0, 2)) {
                            case 'e_':
                            case 'c_':
                                regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                                isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                                break;
                        }
                        break;
                }
            }

            //var reg = new RegExp('(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?', 'i');
            var reg = new RegExp(regExpStr, 'i');
            var idx = curURL.match(reg);
            if (idx != null) {
                var urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                var urlLang = RegExp.$2;
                var urlPara = RegExp.$3;

                //If categories under LatestOnHorse is with E_ or C_, refine the curURL for the lang link in header
                if (isLOHEngChiArt) {                    
                        urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                        urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(curIsEnglish ? '/c_' : '/e_');
			urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(jsPageType.substr(2, jsPageType.length));
			if (jsAction == "list"){
                        	urlPrefix = urlPrefix + '/list';
			}
                        urlLang = RegExp.$3;
                        urlPara = RegExp.$4;                    
                }
                
                if (urlLang == null || urlLang == '' || urlLang.toLowerCase() == '/chinese') {
                    urlLang = '/English';
                }
                else {
                    urlLang = '/Chinese';
                }
                curURL = urlPrefix + urlLang + urlPara;                
            }
            
            $("#topNav a.lang").attr("href", curURL);
        }

        function ajaxNav(url) {
            $.ajax({
                url: url,
                data: { "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest" },
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "html",
                beforeSend: function() {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxBeforeSendTip);
                },
                error: function() {
                    //ajax error
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                },
                success: function(data) {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(data);
                    //for change the language
                    toggleLang(url);
                    //for Image roll over
                    rolloverInit();

                    //not ready for ajax loading
                    if ($('.mainError').length > 0) {

                        curStatus = $("#hidStatus").val();
                        if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                            window.location = url; //refresh the url and use reload approach                                                
                        } else { //ERROR or ...
                            $(".mainError").show();
                            if (curIsSimulcast) {
                                changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                            }
                        }

                    } //endif
                }
            });
        }

        function AutoReload(retryCount) {
            if (retryCount < maxRetryCount) {
                Reload = setTimeout(function() {
                    $.ajax({
                        cache: false,
                        url: preUrl,
                        type: "POST",
                        dataType: "html",
                        error: function() {
                            //ajax error
                            $("#loading").hide();
                            $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                        },
                        success: function(data) {
                            if (data.indexOf("mainError") > 0 && data.indexOf('Redirect') <= 0) {
                                if (data.indexOf('value="ERROR"') > 0) {
                                    retryCount = maxRetryCount;
                                }
                                AutoReload(retryCount + 1);

                            } else {
                                //reset the retry count
                                retryCount = 0;

                                //Data is OK,  and display it!;
                                //Fix the invalidation of js function after update by Ajax
                                window.location = preUrl;
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }, delayTime);
            } else {
                if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                    $(".retryLink").show();
                }

                $("#loading").hide();
                if (hidePanel) {
                    $("#divRemark").show();
                } else {
                    $(".mainError").show();
                    if (curIsSimulcast) {
                        changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                    }
                }
                if (parent.document.location.href.toLowerCase().indexOf(wcmsUrlPrefix) < 0) {
                    try {
                        WATracker.trackPageView('racing-content');
                    } catch (e) {
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
   var focus = "false";
   var search_category = "racing";
   document.getElementById("searchtext").onkeypress = function handleKeyPress(evt){
   var keycode = (window.event)?event.keyCode:evt.which;
	   if(keycode == 13){
		  if(isFocus){
			   focus = "false";
			   goSearch();
			   focus = "true";

		  }
  }
   }
   function replaceAllChar(text, inp) {
	   while(text.indexOf(inp)>=0)
		   text = text.replace(inp, '');
	   return text;
   }
   function goSearch(){

	 if( focus == "false") {

	 var keyword = document.getElementById('searchtext').value;
	 for (var i=0; i<charArr.length; i++)                 
		 keyword = replaceAllChar(keyword, charArr[i]);
	 keyword = keyword.replace(/^\s+/, '').replace(/\s+$/, '');    
	 if(keyword == "" || keyword == "Search" || keyword == "搜尋"){

	 var lang =  "english";
	
	 if(lang == "english")
	alert("Please input a search query");

	 if(lang == "chinese")
			 alert("請輸入搜尋字串");
	}
	else {
		//	+ SearchPath
		  var url = SearchPath + "/search/english/search.aspx?k="+Base64.encode(encodeURIComponent(keyword));
		  if(search_category=="utility"){
			   url += "&g=faq";
		  }
		  else{
			   url += "&g=all";
		  }
		  url += "&t=n";
		  window.location.href = url;
	   }
 }
 else {
		 focus = "false";
	}
 }
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    //add selected effect
    $("#navmenu-h a").filter(function() {
        return this.href.toLowerCase().indexOf("/" + jsController.replace("race", "meeting") + "/" + jsAction) > -1;
    }).addClass("selected");
    //add arrow gif
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").filter(function() {
        return $(this).find("ul").length > 0;
    }).prepend("<div class='navmenu-arrow' />");
    //adjust position of sub menu
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").hover(function() {
        if (document.body.clientWidth < ($(this).offset().left + 400)) {
            $(this).find("ul").css("left", "-101%");
        }
    }, function() {
        $(this).find("ul").css("left", "100%");
    });    
</script>

    <tbody><tr>
        <td>
            <span class="bold">Race 3&nbsp;-&nbsp;WALKER HANDICAP</span>

function getURLType() {
    var url = window.location;
    var localPattern = /racing\/info/i;
    var overseaPattern = /racing\/overseas/i;
    if (localPattern.test(url)) {
        return "local";
    }
    else if (overseaPattern.test(url)) {
        return "overseas";
    }
    else {
        return "na";
    }
}

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var url = "en-us" == "en-us" ? window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "English");

        if ('False' === 'True'){
            url = "/racing/information/English/Horse/SelectHorse.aspx";
        }
        else if ("localresults" == "trackworkonedayresult") {
            url = "/racing/information/English/Trackwork/TrackWorkSearch.aspx";
        }

        $("a.lang").attr("href", ("en-us" == "en-us" ? url.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : url.replace(/English/gi, "English")));
    });

    function ChangeLang() {
        var url = "en-us" == "en-us" ? window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "English");
        if ('False' === 'True') {
            url = "/racing/information/English/Horse/SelectHorse.aspx";
        }
        else if ("localresults" == "trackworkonedayresult") {
            url = "/racing/information/English/Trackwork/TrackWorkSearch.aspx";
        }

        window.location.href = "en-us" == "en-us" ? url.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : url.replace(/English/gi, "English");
    }

    $(function () {

        $("#mainNav .nav .content img").on("mouseover",function () {
            var imgurl = $(this).attr("src");
            var suffix = imgurl.substring(imgurl.lastIndexOf("."), imgurl.length);
            var newimgurl = "";
            if (imgurl.lastIndexOf("_over") < 0) {
                newimgurl = imgurl.substring(0, imgurl.lastIndexOf(".")) + "_over" + suffix;
                $(this).addClass("active");
                $(this).attr("src", newimgurl);
                $(this).attr("delSrc", imgurl);
            }
        })
        $("#mainNav .nav .content img").on("mouseout",function () {
            if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                var imgurl = $(this).attr("delSrc");
                $(this).attr("src", imgurl);
            }
        })

        //$("#mainNav .subNav .content li").on("mouseover",function () {
        //    $(this).siblings().children("a").css("color","#c7b163");
        //    //if (!$(this).find("a").hasClass("active")) {
        //    //    console.log(1)
        //    //    $(this).find("a").addClass("active").parent("li").siblings("li:not(.active)").removeClass("active");
        //    //    $(this).addClass("active");
        //    //}
        //})
        //$("#mainNav .subNav .content li").mouseout(function () {
        //    $(this).siblings().children("a").css("color", "#ae8701");
        //    //if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
        //    //    $(this).removeClass("active");
        //    //    $(this).find("a").removeClass("active");
        //    //}
        //})


        $(".js_twoMenuSelect .menuNav").mouseover(function () {
            $(this).find(".one_nav").addClass("selected");
            $(this).find(".twoMenu").css("visibility", "visible");
        })
        $(".js_twoMenuSelect .menuNav").mouseout(function () {
            $(this).find(".one_nav").removeClass("selected");
            $(this).find(".twoMenu").css("visibility", "hidden");
        })

    })       
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
    var focus = "false";
    var search_category = "racing";
    document.getElementById("searchtext").onkeypress = function handleKeyPress(evt) {
        var keycode = (window.event) ? event.keyCode : evt.which;
        if (keycode == 13) {
            if (isFocus) {
                focus = "false";
                goSearch();
                focus = "true";

            }
        }
    }
    function setSearchVal() {
        document.getElementById('searchkey').value = document.getElementById('searchtext').value;
    }
    function replaceAllChar(text, inp) {
        while (text.indexOf(inp) >= 0)
            text = text.replace(inp, '');
        return text;
    }
    function goSearch() {

        if (focus == "false") {

            var keyword = document.getElementById('searchkey').value;
            for (var i = 0; i < charArr.length; i++)
                keyword = replaceAllChar(keyword, charArr[i]);
            keyword = keyword.replace(/^\s+/, '').replace(/\s+$/, '');
            if (keyword == "") {

                var lang = "english";

                if (lang == "english")
                    alert("Please input a search query");

                if (lang == "chinese")
                    alert("請輸入搜尋字串");
            }
            else {
                var url = "http://search.hkjc.com/search/english/search.aspx?k=" + Base64.encode(encodeURIComponent(keyword));
                if (search_category == "utility") {
                    url += "&g=faq";
                }
                else {
                    url += "&g=all";
                }
                url += "&t=n";
                window.location.href = url;
            }
        }
        else {
            focus = "false";
        }
    }
</script>

                <div class="race_incident_report">
                    <p class="bg_blue font_wb color_w f_fs14">Racing Incident Report</p>
                    <p class="info_p f_fs12">As the start was effected, OSCAR PRINCE became fractious and was slow to begin.  Shortly after the start, BRILLIANT FLASH was steadied away from the heels of BROWN BEAUTY.  Near the 1200 Metres, GALAXEE was steadied when crowded for room inside OSCAR PRINCE which was carried in momentarily by OCTAGONAL CANYON.  After the 1200 Metres, BROWN BEAUTY was checked away from the heels of FANTASTIC GUY.  For some distance after the 400 Metres, WONG'S SUCCESS was steadied when unable to obtain clear running, then over the concluding stages hung in.  At the 300 Metres, GALAXEE was steadied when awkwardly placed inside OSCAR PRINCE which shifted in.  After the 100 Metres, FOREST FOUNTAIN was steadied when disappointed for running between OSCAR PRINCE and ELECTRONICS SPUR.  G Mossé  (GALAXEE) explained after he steadied his mount when crowded for room at the 300 Metres, he then resumed riding GALAXEE out.  He said GALAXEE after having lost its momentum was left flat-footed, however, did manage to make some ground in the concluding stages.  G Mossé was told to ensure he resumes riding his mounts out fully as soon as he is able to in similar circumstances.  When questioned regarding the poor performance of OCTAGONAL CANYON, D Whyte said his mount travelled in a three wide position without cover in the early and middle stages.  He said when SAMBUOYANT improved its position near the 1000 Metres, he endeavoured to follow that horse forward, however, OCTAGONAL CANYON was not travelling well enough to do so.  He said because of this he did not continue to ride OCTAGONAL CANYON to go forward approaching the turn at the 800 Metres.  He said making the turn at the 800 Metres he was able to obtain a position with cover on OCTAGONAL CANYON, however, his mount when placed under pressure prior to straightening did not respond to his riding.  OCTAGONAL CANYON was sent for an official veterinary inspection and sampling.  FANTASTIC GUY and HAPPY ALL AROUND were sent for an official veterinary inspection.  A veterinary inspection of OCTAGONAL CANYON and FANTASTIC GUY after the race did not show any significant findings.  After the race, HAPPY ALL AROUND was examined by the Veterinary Officer.  He said an endoscopic examination showed a substantial amount of blood in the horse's trachea.  Before being allowed to race again, HAPPY ALL AROUND will be subjected to an official veterinary examination.  SAMBUOYANT and ZEPHYRUS were sent for sampling.  After the race, the Veterinary Officer reported SAMBUOYANT had lost its left front plate.</p>

    $(function () {
        $(".js_racecard img").mouseover(function () {
            var imgurl = $(this).attr("src");
            var suffix = imgurl.substring(imgurl.lastIndexOf("."), imgurl.length);
            var newimgurl = "";
            if (imgurl.indexOf("_o") < 0) {
                newimgurl = imgurl.substring(0, imgurl.lastIndexOf(".")) + "_r" + suffix;
                $(this).addClass("active");
                $(this).attr("src", newimgurl);
                $(this).attr("delSrc", imgurl);
            }
        })
        $(".js_racecard img").mouseout(function () {
            if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                var imgurl = $(this).attr("delSrc");
                $(this).attr("src", imgurl);
            }
        })

        $("#submitBtn").click(function () {
            var raceDate = $("#selectId").val();
            var raceDate1 = raceDate.toString().split('/').reverse().join('/');

            window.location.href = "/racing/information/English/Racing/LocalResults.aspx?RaceDate=" + raceDate1;
        })
    })

    }

<script type="text/javascript">
			
			function jcew_getDynamicCurrentOddsUrl(link, isPopup) {
				var param = 'na';
				var url = window.location;
				var localPattern = /racing\/info/i;
				var overseaPattern = /racing\/overseas/i;
				if(localPattern.test(url)){
					param = 'local';
				}
				else if(overseaPattern.test(url)){
					param = 'overseas';
				}
						
				var newLink = link + '&dv=' + param;
				if (isPopup) {
				  window.open(newLink, '_blank');
				} else {
				  window.location.href = newLink;
				}
			}

    <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">var HkjcWebUrl = '//www.hkjc.com';
var JcrwUrlPrefix = '/racing/Info';
var ajaxBeforeSendTip = '<div style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; text-align:center;">Processing...</div><br/>';
var ajaxErrorTip = '<div style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; text-align:center;">Network or system busy, please try again later. Sorry for the inconveniences caused.</div><br/>';
var jsController = 'race';

var maxRetryCount = 4;

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var curStatus = null;

        function toggleLang() {
            var curURL = document.URL;  //document.location.href;
            var isLOHEngChiArt = false; //Check if it is E_ or C_ type categories 
            if (arguments.length > 0) {
                curURL = arguments[0];
            }

            var regExpStr = '(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
            if (jsController == 'latestonhorse') {
                switch (jsAction) {
                    case 'index':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        break;
                    case 'show':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/tp50|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/csum|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/smon|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/clas)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';

			if (curURL.indexOf('_ahrl') >= 0) {
                            regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/[e|c]_ahrl)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                            jsPageType = curURL.indexOf('e_ahrl') ? 'e_ahrl' : 'c_ahrl';
                            isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                        }

                        break;
                    case 'list':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        switch (jsPageType.substr(0, 2)) {
                            case 'e_':
                            case 'c_':
                                regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                                isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                                break;
                        }
                        break;
                }
            }

            //var reg = new RegExp('(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?', 'i');
            var reg = new RegExp(regExpStr, 'i');
            var idx = curURL.match(reg);
            if (idx != null) {
                var urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                var urlLang = RegExp.$2;
                var urlPara = RegExp.$3;

                //If categories under LatestOnHorse is with E_ or C_, refine the curURL for the lang link in header
                if (isLOHEngChiArt) {                    
                        urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                        urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(curIsEnglish ? '/c_' : '/e_');
			urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(jsPageType.substr(2, jsPageType.length));
			if (jsAction == "list"){
                        	urlPrefix = urlPrefix + '/list';
			}
                        urlLang = RegExp.$3;
                        urlPara = RegExp.$4;                    
                }
                
                if (urlLang == null || urlLang == '' || urlLang.toLowerCase() == '/chinese') {
                    urlLang = '/English';
                }
                else {
                    urlLang = '/Chinese';
                }
                curURL = urlPrefix + urlLang + urlPara;                
            }
            
            $("#topNav a.lang").attr("href", curURL);
        }

        function ajaxNav(url) {
            $.ajax({
                url: url,
                data: { "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest" },
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "html",
                beforeSend: function() {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxBeforeSendTip);
                },
                error: function() {
                    //ajax error
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                },
                success: function(data) {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(data);
                    //for change the language
                    toggleLang(url);
                    //for Image roll over
                    rolloverInit();

                    //not ready for ajax loading
                    if ($('.mainError').length > 0) {

                        curStatus = $("#hidStatus").val();
                        if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                            window.location = url; //refresh the url and use reload approach                                                
                        } else { //ERROR or ...
                            $(".mainError").show();
                            if (curIsSimulcast) {
                                changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                            }
                        }

                    } //endif
                }
            });
        }

        function AutoReload(retryCount) {
            if (retryCount < maxRetryCount) {
                Reload = setTimeout(function() {
                    $.ajax({
                        cache: false,
                        url: preUrl,
                        type: "POST",
                        dataType: "html",
                        error: function() {
                            //ajax error
                            $("#loading").hide();
                            $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                        },
                        success: function(data) {
                            if (data.indexOf("mainError") > 0 && data.indexOf('Redirect') <= 0) {
                                if (data.indexOf('value="ERROR"') > 0) {
                                    retryCount = maxRetryCount;
                                }
                                AutoReload(retryCount + 1);

                            } else {
                                //reset the retry count
                                retryCount = 0;

                                //Data is OK,  and display it!;
                                //Fix the invalidation of js function after update by Ajax
                                window.location = preUrl;
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }, delayTime);
            } else {
                if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                    $(".retryLink").show();
                }

                $("#loading").hide();
                if (hidePanel) {
                    $("#divRemark").show();
                } else {
                    $(".mainError").show();
                    if (curIsSimulcast) {
                        changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                    }
                }
                if (parent.document.location.href.toLowerCase().indexOf(wcmsUrlPrefix) < 0) {
                    try {
                        WATracker.trackPageView('racing-content');
                    } catch (e) {
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

</head>

<!-- script for search box -->
<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
   var focus = "false";
   var search_category = "racing";
   document.getElementById("searchtext").onkeypress = function handleKeyPress(evt){
   var keycode = (window.event)?event.keyCode:evt.which;
	   if(keycode == 13){
		  if(isFocus){
			   focus = "false";
			   goSearch();
			   focus = "true";

		  }
  }
   }
   function replaceAllChar(text, inp) {
	   while(text.indexOf(inp)>=0)
		   text = text.replace(inp, '');
	   return text;
   }
   function goSearch(){

	 if( focus == "false") {

	 var keyword = document.getElementById('searchtext').value;
	 for (var i=0; i<charArr.length; i++)                 
		 keyword = replaceAllChar(keyword, charArr[i]);
	 keyword = keyword.replace(/^\s+/, '').replace(/\s+$/, '');    
	 if(keyword == "" || keyword == "Search" || keyword == "搜尋"){

	 var lang =  "english";
	
	 if(lang == "english")
	alert("Please input a search query");

	 if(lang == "chinese")
			 alert("請輸入搜尋字串");
	}
	else {
		//	+ SearchPath
		  var url = SearchPath + "/search/english/search.aspx?k="+Base64.encode(encodeURIComponent(keyword));
		  if(search_category=="utility"){
			   url += "&g=faq";
		  }
		  else{
			   url += "&g=all";
		  }
		  url += "&t=n";
		  window.location.href = url;
	   }
 }
 else {
		 focus = "false";
	}
 }
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    //add selected effect
    $("#navmenu-h a").filter(function() {
        return this.href.toLowerCase().indexOf("/" + jsController.replace("race", "meeting") + "/" + jsAction) > -1;
    }).addClass("selected");
    //add arrow gif
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").filter(function() {
        return $(this).find("ul").length > 0;
    }).prepend("<div class='navmenu-arrow' />");
    //adjust position of sub menu
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").hover(function() {
        if (document.body.clientWidth < ($(this).offset().left + 400)) {
            $(this).find("ul").css("left", "-101%");
        }
    }, function() {
        $(this).find("ul").css("left", "100%");
    });    
</script>

        $("select").css("visibility", "hidden");
    }, function() {
        $("select").css("visibility", "visible");
    });
    //add iehover effect for IE6
    $("#navmenu-h li").hover(function() {
        $(this).addClass("iehover");
    }, function() {
        $(this).removeClass("iehover");
    });
</script>
<![endif]-->

<script type="text/javascript">
    function OpenWin(site, fileName) {
        var url = site + '/racing/racecourse_img.asp?filename=' + fileName;
        var newWin = window.open(url, 'ShowHorsePic', 'top=200 screenX=200, left=300 screenY=300, width=500,height=353,resizable=0,scrollbar=1,menubar=0,toolbar=0')
        if (window.newWin) {
            newWin.focus()
        }
    }

    function MM_openBrWindow(theURL, winName, features) {
        window.open(theURL, winName, features);
    }

    function openEasyformShortcut(easyformPath, raceNo, displayLang) {
        if (screen.availHeight >= 700) {
            var easyform = window.open(easyformPath + "?shortcut=30&raceNo=" + raceNo + "&lang=" + displayLang, "easyform", "toolbar=no,location=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,screenX=0,screenY=0,left=0,top=0,maximize=1");
        }
        else {
            var easyform = window.open(easyformPath + "?shortcut=30&raceNo=" + raceNo + "&lang=" + displayLang, "easyform", "toolbar=no,location=no,status=no,menubar=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=no,screenX=0,screenY=0,left=0,top=0,maximize=1");
        }
        easyform.focus();
    } 
</script>

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
    function OpenPopWinScroll(ps_Link, pv_Width, pv_Height, ps_Win) {
        var pv_Left = 20;
        var pv_Top = 20;
        var ls_options = "status=no,toolbar=no,menubar=no,location=no,scrollbars=yes,resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,left=" + pv_Left + ",top=" + pv_Top + ",width=" + pv_Width + ",height=" + pv_Height;
        window.open(ps_Link, ps_Win, ls_options);
    }
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">

function getURLType() {
    var url = window.location;
    var localPattern = /racing\/info/i;
    var overseaPattern = /racing\/overseas/i;
    if (localPattern.test(url)) {
        return "local";
    }
    else if (overseaPattern.test(url)) {
        return "overseas";
    }
    else {
        return "na";
    }
}

document.write('' + 
'<div id="seo" class="fiveCol">' +
'<div class="content clearfix">' +
'<dl>' +

        $(document).ready(function () {

            $(".js_racecard_rt_num img").on("mouseover", function () {
                var imgurl = $(this).attr("src");
                var suffix = imgurl.substring(imgurl.lastIndexOf("."), imgurl.length);
                var newimgurl = "";
                if (imgurl.lastIndexOf("_o") < 0) {
                    newimgurl = imgurl.substring(0, imgurl.lastIndexOf(".")) + "_r" + suffix;
                    $(this).addClass("active");
                    $(this).attr("src", newimgurl);
                    $(this).attr("delSrc", imgurl);
                }
            })
            $(".js_racecard_rt_num img").on("mouseout", function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                    var imgurl = $(this).attr("delSrc");
                    $(this).attr("src", imgurl);
                }
            })

            $(".js_racecard_btn a img").on("mouseover", function () {
                var imgurl = $(this).attr("src");
                var suffix = imgurl.substring(imgurl.lastIndexOf("."), imgurl.length);
                var newimgurl = "";
                if (imgurl.lastIndexOf("_o") < 0) {
                    newimgurl = imgurl.substring(0, imgurl.lastIndexOf(".")) + "_r" + suffix;
                    $(this).addClass("active");
                    $(this).attr("src", newimgurl);
                    $(this).attr("delSrc", imgurl);
                }
            })
            $(".js_racecard_btn a img").on("mouseout", function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                    var imgurl = $(this).attr("delSrc");
                    $(this).attr("src", imgurl);
                }
            })

            $("img[id^=racecard_v3_btn][id$=_r]").mouseover(function () {
                var imgurl = $(this).attr("src");
                var suffix = imgurl.substring(imgurl.lastIndexOf("."), imgurl.length);
                var newimgurl = "";
                if (imgurl.indexOf("_r") < 0) {
                    newimgurl = imgurl.substring(0, imgurl.lastIndexOf(".")) + "_r" + suffix;
                    $(this).addClass("active");
                    $(this).attr("src", newimgurl);
                    $(this).attr("delSrc", imgurl);
                }
            })
            $("img[id^=racecard_v3_btn][id$=_r]").mouseout(function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                    var imgurl = $(this).attr("delSrc");
                    $(this).attr("src", imgurl);
                }
            })

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var url = "en-us" == "en-us" ? window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "English");

        if ('False' === 'True'){
            url = "/racing/information/English/Horse/SelectHorse.aspx";
        }
        else if ("localtrackwork" == "trackworkonedayresult") {
            url = "/racing/information/English/Trackwork/TrackWorkSearch.aspx";
        }

        $("a.lang").attr("href", ("en-us" == "en-us" ? url.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : url.replace(/English/gi, "English")));
    });

    function ChangeLang() {
        var url = "en-us" == "en-us" ? window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : window.location.href.replace(/English/gi, "English");
        if ('False' === 'True') {
            url = "/racing/information/English/Horse/SelectHorse.aspx";
        }
        else if ("localtrackwork" == "trackworkonedayresult") {
            url = "/racing/information/English/Trackwork/TrackWorkSearch.aspx";
        }

        window.location.href = "en-us" == "en-us" ? url.replace(/English/gi, "Chinese") : url.replace(/English/gi, "English");
    }

    $(function () {

        $("#mainNav .nav .content img").on("mouseover",function () {
            var imgurl = $(this).attr("src");
            var suffix = imgurl.substring(imgurl.lastIndexOf("."), imgurl.length);
            var newimgurl = "";
            if (imgurl.lastIndexOf("_over") < 0) {
                newimgurl = imgurl.substring(0, imgurl.lastIndexOf(".")) + "_over" + suffix;
                $(this).addClass("active");
                $(this).attr("src", newimgurl);
                $(this).attr("delSrc", imgurl);
            }
        })
        $("#mainNav .nav .content img").on("mouseout",function () {
            if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                var imgurl = $(this).attr("delSrc");
                $(this).attr("src", imgurl);
            }
        })

        //$("#mainNav .subNav .content li").on("mouseover",function () {
        //    $(this).siblings().children("a").css("color","#c7b163");
        //    //if (!$(this).find("a").hasClass("active")) {
        //    //    console.log(1)
        //    //    $(this).find("a").addClass("active").parent("li").siblings("li:not(.active)").removeClass("active");
        //    //    $(this).addClass("active");
        //    //}
        //})
        //$("#mainNav .subNav .content li").mouseout(function () {
        //    $(this).siblings().children("a").css("color", "#ae8701");
        //    //if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
        //    //    $(this).removeClass("active");
        //    //    $(this).find("a").removeClass("active");
        //    //}
        //})


        $(".js_twoMenuSelect .menuNav").mouseover(function () {
            $(this).find(".one_nav").addClass("selected");
            $(this).find(".twoMenu").css("visibility", "visible");
        })
        $(".js_twoMenuSelect .menuNav").mouseout(function () {
            $(this).find(".one_nav").removeClass("selected");
            $(this).find(".twoMenu").css("visibility", "hidden");
        })

    })       
</script>

    setTimeout(showLogin, 25);

<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
    var focus = "false";
    var search_category = "racing";
    document.getElementById("searchtext").onkeypress = function handleKeyPress(evt) {
        var keycode = (window.event) ? event.keyCode : evt.which;
        if (keycode == 13) {
            if (isFocus) {
                focus = "false";
                goSearch();
                focus = "true";

            }
        }
    }
    function setSearchVal() {
        document.getElementById('searchkey').value = document.getElementById('searchtext').value;
    }
    function replaceAllChar(text, inp) {
        while (text.indexOf(inp) >= 0)
            text = text.replace(inp, '');
        return text;
    }
    function goSearch() {

        if (focus == "false") {

            var keyword = document.getElementById('searchkey').value;
            for (var i = 0; i < charArr.length; i++)
                keyword = replaceAllChar(keyword, charArr[i]);
            keyword = keyword.replace(/^\s+/, '').replace(/\s+$/, '');
            if (keyword == "") {

                var lang = "english";

                if (lang == "english")
                    alert("Please input a search query");

                if (lang == "chinese")
                    alert("請輸入搜尋字串");
            }
            else {
                var url = "http://search.hkjc.com/search/english/search.aspx?k=" + Base64.encode(encodeURIComponent(keyword));
                if (search_category == "utility") {
                    url += "&g=faq";
                }
                else {
                    url += "&g=all";
                }
                url += "&t=n";
                window.location.href = url;
            }
        }
        else {
            focus = "false";
        }
    }
</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $(".subNav").find("li").each(function () {
                    if ($(this).children("a:first").text() == "Racing Info (Local)") {
                        var secondNav = $(this).children("a:first").siblings("div[class='pullmenu clearfix']:first").children("div[class='content']");
                        $("#header_bottom_banner").html(secondNav.html());
                        $("#header_bottom_banner dl").addClass("f_clear");
                        // $("#header_bottom_banner dl").append("<dt style='clear:both'></dt>");
                        $("#header_bottom_banner>dl>dt>a").each(function () {
                            $(this).prev().hide();
                            var a_parent = $(this).parent();
                            a_parent.mouseover(function () {
                                var thirdNavDiv = $(this).children("div:first");
                                thirdNavDiv.show();
                                thirdNavDiv.attr("id", "third_nav");
                                thirdNavDiv.removeClass();
                            });
                            a_parent.mouseout(function () {
                                $(this).children("div:first").hide();
                            });

                        });

                    }
                });
            });
        </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
			
			function jcew_getDynamicCurrentOddsUrl(link, isPopup) {
				var param = 'na';
				var url = window.location;
				var localPattern = /racing\/info/i;
				var overseaPattern = /racing\/overseas/i;
				if(localPattern.test(url)){
					param = 'local';
				}
				else if(overseaPattern.test(url)){
					param = 'overseas';
				}
						
				var newLink = link + '&dv=' + param;
				if (isPopup) {
				  window.open(newLink, '_blank');
				} else {
				  window.location.href = newLink;
				}
			}
			
		</script><div id="seo" class="fiveCol">

    <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">var HkjcWebUrl = '//www.hkjc.com';
var JcrwUrlPrefix = '/racing/Info';
var ajaxBeforeSendTip = '<div style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; text-align:center;">Processing...</div><br/>';
var ajaxErrorTip = '<div style="font-size:14px; font-weight:bold; text-align:center;">Network or system busy, please try again later. Sorry for the inconveniences caused.</div><br/>';
var jsController = 'race';
var jsAction = 'veterinaryrecord';
var jsJcerwWebUrl = '//racing.hkjc.com/racing/info';
var jsJCRWDomainIP = 'racing.hkjc.com';
var jsJCEWDomainIP = 'www.hkjc.com';

var wcmsUrlPrefix = '//racing.hkjc.com/racing/overseas';
var preUrl = '/racing/info/meeting/VeterinaryRecord/English/Local/20090118/ST/03';
var maxRetryCount = 4;
var delayTime = '2000';
var JcrwSSOPath = '//racing.hkjc.com/racing/jcrw/';

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var curStatus = null;

        function toggleLang() {
            var curURL = document.URL;  //document.location.href;
            var isLOHEngChiArt = false; //Check if it is E_ or C_ type categories 
            if (arguments.length > 0) {
                curURL = arguments[0];
            }

            var regExpStr = '(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
            if (jsController == 'latestonhorse') {
                switch (jsAction) {
                    case 'index':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        break;
                    case 'show':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/tp50|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/csum|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/smon|.*\\/latestonhorse\\/clas)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';

			if (curURL.indexOf('_ahrl') >= 0) {
                            regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/[e|c]_ahrl)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                            jsPageType = curURL.indexOf('e_ahrl') ? 'e_ahrl' : 'c_ahrl';
                            isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                        }

                        break;
                    case 'list':
                        regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                        switch (jsPageType.substr(0, 2)) {
                            case 'e_':
                            case 'c_':
                                regExpStr = '(.*\\/latestonhorse)(\\/.*\\/list)(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?';
                                isLOHEngChiArt = true;
                                break;
                        }
                        break;
                }
            }

            //var reg = new RegExp('(.*\\/' + jsAction + ')(\\/English|\\/Chinese)?(\\/.*)?', 'i');
            var reg = new RegExp(regExpStr, 'i');
            var idx = curURL.match(reg);
            if (idx != null) {
                var urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                var urlLang = RegExp.$2;
                var urlPara = RegExp.$3;

                //If categories under LatestOnHorse is with E_ or C_, refine the curURL for the lang link in header
                if (isLOHEngChiArt) {                    
                        urlPrefix = RegExp.$1;
                        urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(curIsEnglish ? '/c_' : '/e_');
			urlPrefix = urlPrefix.concat(jsPageType.substr(2, jsPageType.length));
			if (jsAction == "list"){
                        	urlPrefix = urlPrefix + '/list';
			}
                        urlLang = RegExp.$3;
                        urlPara = RegExp.$4;                    
                }
                
                if (urlLang == null || urlLang == '' || urlLang.toLowerCase() == '/chinese') {
                    urlLang = '/English';
                }
                else {
                    urlLang = '/Chinese';
                }
                curURL = urlPrefix + urlLang + urlPara;                
            }
            
            $("#topNav a.lang").attr("href", curURL);
        }

        function ajaxNav(url) {
            $.ajax({
                url: url,
                data: { "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest" },
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "html",
                beforeSend: function() {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxBeforeSendTip);
                },
                error: function() {
                    //ajax error
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                },
                success: function(data) {
                    $('#' + jsAction).html(data);
                    //for change the language
                    toggleLang(url);
                    //for Image roll over
                    rolloverInit();

                    //not ready for ajax loading
                    if ($('.mainError').length > 0) {

                        curStatus = $("#hidStatus").val();
                        if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                            window.location = url; //refresh the url and use reload approach                                                
                        } else { //ERROR or ...
                            $(".mainError").show();
                            if (curIsSimulcast) {
                                changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                            }
                        }

                    } //endif
                }
            });
        }

        function AutoReload(retryCount) {
            if (retryCount < maxRetryCount) {
                Reload = setTimeout(function() {
                    $.ajax({
                        cache: false,
                        url: preUrl,
                        type: "POST",
                        dataType: "html",
                        error: function() {
                            //ajax error
                            $("#loading").hide();
                            $('#' + jsAction).html(ajaxErrorTip);
                        },
                        success: function(data) {
                            if (data.indexOf("mainError") > 0 && data.indexOf('Redirect') <= 0) {
                                if (data.indexOf('value="ERROR"') > 0) {
                                    retryCount = maxRetryCount;
                                }
                                AutoReload(retryCount + 1);

                            } else {
                                //reset the retry count
                                retryCount = 0;

                                //Data is OK,  and display it!;
                                //Fix the invalidation of js function after update by Ajax
                                window.location = preUrl;
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }, delayTime);
            } else {
                if (curStatus == "NOTREADY") {
                    $(".retryLink").show();
                }

                $("#loading").hide();
                if (hidePanel) {
                    $("#divRemark").show();
                } else {
                    $(".mainError").show();
                    if (curIsSimulcast) {
                        changeIFrameSize("sysdata_iframe");
                    }
                }
                if (parent.document.location.href.toLowerCase().indexOf(wcmsUrlPrefix) < 0) {
                    try {
                        WATracker.trackPageView('racing-content');
                    } catch (e) {
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

<!-- script for search box -->
<script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
   var focus = "false";
   var search_category = "racing";
   document.getElementById("searchtext").onkeypress = function handleKeyPress(evt){
   var keycode = (window.event)?event.keyCode:evt.which;
	   if(keycode == 13){
		  if(isFocus){
			   focus = "false";
			   goSearch();
			   focus = "true";

		  }
  }
   }
   function replaceAllChar(text, inp) {
	   while(text.indexOf(inp)>=0)
		   text = text.replace(inp, '');
	   return text;
   }
   function goSearch(){

	 if( focus == "false") {

	 var keyword = document.getElementById('searchtext').value;
	 for (var i=0; i<charArr.length; i++)                 
		 keyword = replaceAllChar(keyword, charArr[i]);
	 keyword = keyword.replace(/^\s+/, '').replace(/\s+$/, '');    
	 if(keyword == "" || keyword == "Search" || keyword == "搜尋"){

	 var lang =  "english";
	
	 if(lang == "english")
	alert("Please input a search query");

	 if(lang == "chinese")
			 alert("請輸入搜尋字串");
	}
	else {
		//	+ SearchPath
		  var url = SearchPath + "/search/english/search.aspx?k="+Base64.encode(encodeURIComponent(keyword));
		  if(search_category=="utility"){
			   url += "&g=faq";
		  }
		  else{
			   url += "&g=all";
		  }
		  url += "&t=n";
		  window.location.href = url;
	   }
 }
 else {
		 focus = "false";
	}
 }
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
    //add selected effect
    $("#navmenu-h a").filter(function() {
        return this.href.toLowerCase().indexOf("/" + jsController.replace("race", "meeting") + "/" + jsAction) > -1;
    }).addClass("selected");
    //add arrow gif
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").filter(function() {
        return $(this).find("ul").length > 0;
    }).prepend("<div class='navmenu-arrow' />");
    //adjust position of sub menu
    $("#navmenu-h>li li").hover(function() {
        if (document.body.clientWidth < ($(this).offset().left + 400)) {
            $(this).find("ul").css("left", "-101%");
        }
    }, function() {
        $(this).find("ul").css("left", "100%");
    });    
</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">

function getURLType() {
    var url = window.location;
    var localPattern = /racing\/info/i;
    var overseaPattern = /racing\/overseas/i;
    if (localPattern.test(url)) {
        return "local";
    }
    else if (overseaPattern.test(url)) {
        return "overseas";
    }
    else {
        return "na";
    }
}

document.write('' + 
'<div id="seo" class="fiveCol">' +
